has_competitors flag based on derived competitors --- #}\\nCompetitorCheck AS (\\n    SELECT COUNT(*) > 0 AS has_any FROM DerivedCompetitors\\n)\\n,\\nAllBrands AS (\\n    -- Define Target Brand (Use Score', 'Beat Score')\\n),\\nStartEndPositioning AS (\\n    -- Get positioning data for relevant brands at start and end dates\\n    SELECT p.*, ab.is_target_brand\\n    FROM positioning p\\n    JOIN ========================= #}\\n\\nMetricChanges AS (\\n    -- Calculate changes for Pulse Score, Beat Scores, and Rank\\n    SELECT\\n        brand,\\n        is_target_brand,\\n        score_type,\\n        brand_pulse_component, -- Will be NULL for Pulse Score\\n        MAX(CASE WHEN month_start_date = dp.end_date THEN score END) AS end_score,\\n        MAX(CASE WHEN month_start_date = dp.start_date THEN score END) AS start_score,\\n        (MAX(CASE WHEN month_start_date = dp.end_date THEN score END) - MAX(CASE WHEN month_start_date = dp.start_date THEN score END)) AS score_change,\\n        MAX(CASE WHEN month_start_date = dp.end_date THEN score_rank END) AS end_rank,\\n        MAX(CASE WHEN month_start_date = dp.start_date THEN score_rank END) AS start_rank,\\n        -- Rank Improvement: Positive means rank got better (lower number)\\n        (MAX(CASE WHEN month_start_date = dp.start_date THEN score_rank END) - MAX(CASE WHEN month_start_date = dp.end_date THEN score_rank END)) AS rank_improvement\\n    FROM StartEndSummary\\n    CROSS JOIN DateParams dp\\n    GROUP BY brand, is_target_brand, score_type, brand_pulse_component\\n),\\nPositioningChanges AS (\\n    -- Calculate changes for Positioning attributes\\n    SELECT\\n        brand,\\n        is_target_brand,\\n        attributes,\\n        MAX(CASE WHEN month_start_date = dp.end_date THEN score END) AS end_score,\\n        MAX(CASE WHEN month_start_date = dp.start_date THEN score END) AS start_score,\\n        (MAX(CASE WHEN month_start_date = dp.end_date THEN score END) - MAX(CASE WHEN month_start_date = dp.start_date THEN score END)) AS score_change\\n    FROM StartEndPositioning\\n    CROSS JOIN DateParams dp\\n    GROUP BY brand, is_target_brand, attributes\\n),\\n\\n{# flag\\n-- We'll use Jinja to conditionally include them if needed later, or handle NULLs in joins\\n,\\nCompetitorChanges AS (\\n    -- Isolate changes for competitors (only relevant if  LEFT JOIN AvgCompPositioningChange acpc ON tpc.attributes = acpc.attributes -- LEFT JOIN handles no competitors\\n    WHERE tpc.start_score IS NOT NULL OR tpc.end_score IS NOT NULL -- Changed to OR NOT NULL\\n      AND c.start_rank > t.start_rank AND c.end_rank < t.end_rank -- Comp started worse, ended better\\n    LIMIT {{ top_n_competitors | int }}\\n)\\n,\\n{# ======================== CTEs for Top/Bottom Drivers ========================= #}\\n\\nTopPositiveDrivers AS (\\n     SELECT brand_pulse_component, start_score, end_score, score_change\\n     FROM TargetChanges\\n     WHERE ============================ #}\\n\\n-- Define the final combined data as the last CTE in the sequence\\n, FinalSWOTData AS (\\n    -- Combine Core Metrics (Pulse & Beat Scores) for Target Brand\\n  -- Derive SWOT Category based on metric changes\\n        CASE\\n            WHEN tc.score_type = 'Pulse Score' AND tc.score_change > 0 THEN 'Strength'\\n            WHEN tc.score_type = 'Pulse Score' AND tc.score_change < 0 THEN 'Weakness'\\n            WHEN tc.score_type = 'Pulse Score' AND tc.rank_improvement > 0 THEN 'Strength' -- Rank Improved\\n            WHEN tc.score_type = 'Pulse Score' AND tc.rank_improvement < 0 THEN 'Weakness' -- Rank Declined\\n            WHEN tc.score_type = 'Beat Score' AND tc.score_change > 0 THEN 'Strength'\\n            WHEN tc.score_type = 'Beat Score' AND tc.score_change < 0 THEN 'Weakness'\\n            ELSE NULL -- Default if no clear S/W based on score/rank change\\n        END AS swot_category,\\n        -- Derive Finding Description\\n        CASE\\n            WHEN tc.score_type = 'Pulse Score' AND tc.score_change > 0 THEN 'Pulse score grew over the period.'\\n            WHEN tc.score_type = 'Pulse Score' AND tc.score_change < 0 THEN 'Pulse score declined over the period.'\\n            WHEN tc.score_type = 'Pulse Score' AND tc.rank_improvement > 0 THEN 'Pulse score rank improved.'\\n            WHEN tc.score_type = 'Pulse Score' AND tc.rank_improvement < 0 THEN 'Pulse score rank declined.'\\n            WHEN tc.score_type = 'Beat Score' AND tc.score_change > 0 THEN tc.brand_pulse_component || ' beat score grew.'\\n            WHEN tc.score_type = 'Beat Score' AND tc.score_change < 0 THEN tc.brand_pulse_component || ' beat score declined.'\\n            ELSE 'Overall metric value'\\n        END AS finding_description,\\n        -- Construct Factual Basis string\\n        'Start: ' || COALESCE(ROUND(tc.start_score, 2)::VARCHAR, 'N/A') ||\\n        ', End: ' || COALESCE(ROUND(tc.end_score, 2)::VARCHAR, 'N/A') ||\\n        ', Change: ' || COALESCE(ROUND(tc.score_change, 2)::VARCHAR, 'N/A') ||\\n        -- Include rank info only if it was calculated (i.e., if competitors exist)\\n        CASE WHEN tc.start_rank IS NOT NULL THEN\\n            ', Start Rank: ' || tc.start_rank::VARCHAR || ', End Rank: ' || tc.end_rank::VARCHAR ||\\n            ', Rank Improvement: ' || tc.rank_improvement::VARCHAR\\n            ELSE '' END\\n        AS factual_basis\\n    FROM TargetChanges tc\\n    CROSS JOIN DateParams dp\\n    WHERE tc.start_score IS NOT NULL OR tc.end_score IS NOT NULL -- Include if data exists for either start or end\\n\\n    UNION ALL\\n    -- SWOT Findings from Positioning Analysis (uses LEFT JOIN, runs even w/o competitors)\\n    SELECT\\n        dp.start_date::VARCHAR, dp.end_date::VARCHAR, '{{ brand_name }}', -- Use pre-escaped brand_name\\n        'Positioning', NULL, tpa.attributes,\\n        ROUND(tpa.target_start_score, 2), ROUND(tpa.target_end_score, 2), ROUND(tpa.target_score_change, 2),\\n        NULL, NULL, NULL, -- Ranks not applicable to positioning\\n        -- Derive SWOT for Positioning (Handles NULLs from LEFT JOIN if no comps)\\n        CASE\\n            -- Strength: Gained significant advantage or maintained high advantage\\n            WHEN tpa.end_advantage >= {{ positioning_advantage_threshold | float }} AND tpa.target_score_change >= 0 THEN 'Strength'\\n            -- Weakness: Lost significant advantage or has significant disadvantage\\n            WHEN tpa.start_advantage >= {{ positioning_advantage_threshold | float }} AND tpa.end_advantage < {{ positioning_advantage_threshold | float }} THEN 'Weakness'\\n            WHEN tpa.end_advantage <= -{{ positioning_advantage_threshold | float }} THEN 'Weakness'\\n            -- Opportunity: Potential to gain advantage where competitors are weak/declining or target is improving\\n            WHEN tpa.target_score_change > 0 AND COALESCE(tpa.target_score_change > tpa.avg_comp_score_change, TRUE) THEN 'Opportunity'\\n            -- Threat: Losing advantage or competitors gaining faster\\n            WHEN tpa.target_score_change < 0 AND COALESCE(tpa.target_score_change < tpa.avg_comp_score_change, TRUE) THEN 'Threat'\\n            WHEN tpa.end_advantage < tpa.start_advantage THEN 'Threat' -- Losing relative ground\\n            ELSE NULL\\n        END AS swot_category,\\n        -- Description for Positioning\\n        CASE\\n            WHEN tpa.end_advantage >= {{ positioning_advantage_threshold | float }} AND tpa.target_score_change >= 0 THEN 'Maintained/Gained strong advantage in ' || tpa.attributes\\n            WHEN tpa.start_advantage >= {{ positioning_advantage_threshold | float }} AND tpa.end_advantage < {{ positioning_advantage_threshold | float }} THEN 'Lost significant advantage in ' || tpa.attributes\\n            WHEN tpa.end_advantage <= -{{ positioning_advantage_threshold | float }} THEN 'Significant disadvantage in ' || tpa.attributes\\n            WHEN tpa.target_score_change > 0 AND COALESCE(tpa.target_score_change > tpa.avg_comp_score_change, TRUE) THEN 'Improving faster than avg competitor on ' || tpa.attributes\\n            WHEN tpa.target_score_change < 0 AND COALESCE(tpa.target_score_change < tpa.avg_comp_score_change, TRUE) THEN 'Declining faster than avg competitor on ' || tpa.attributes\\n            WHEN tpa.end_advantage < tpa.start_advantage THEN 'Losing relative advantage in ' || tpa.attributes\\n            ELSE 'Positioning change for ' || tpa.attributes\\n        END AS finding_description,\\n        -- Factual Basis for Positioning\\n        'Target Start: ' || ROUND(tpa.target_start_score, 2)::VARCHAR || ', Target End: ' || ROUND(tpa.target_end_score, 2)::VARCHAR ||\\n        ', Target Change: ' || ROUND(tpa.target_score_change, 2)::VARCHAR ||\\n        -- Only show competitor avg info if it exists\\n        CASE WHEN tpa.avg_comp_start_score IS NOT NULL THEN\\n            ', Comp Avg Start: ' || ROUND(tpa.avg_comp_start_score, 2)::VARCHAR ||\\n            ', Comp Avg End: ' || ROUND(tpa.avg_comp_end_score, 2)::VARCHAR\\n            ELSE '' END ||\\n        ', Start Adv: ' || ROUND(tpa.start_advantage, 2)::VARCHAR || ', End Adv: ' || ROUND(tpa.end_advantage, 2)::VARCHAR\\n        AS factual_basis\\n    FROM TargetPositioningAnalysis tpa\\n    CROSS JOIN DateParams dp\\n\\n
